MORA (SAT) 08/16/1986 Palacio de los Deportes, Iztacalco, Distrito Federal [https://www.facebook.com/LuchaLibreDeAyerdeHoyYSiempre/posts/915097345204668 DJ Spectro]
&& El Santo vs Kato Kung Lee was scheduled to take place - but the ring didn't arrive. The promotion realized it had no ring late and scrambled to get a replacement one, but the commission only gave them 30 minutes from scheduled show time to start or they'd have to refund everyone. A replacement ring arrived, but too late, and Promociones Mora took a huge loss. Magazines later claimed the people responisble from bringing the ring were paid off not to show by a rival promoter (though not EMLL); Mora denied the story but promoted mostly in Tijuana going forward.
